FNV PBR CLOSE TERRAIN PASS IDENTITY FOLLOWUP

Goal:
- Find a positive identity key for true close landscape base/alpha draws.
- Prove exclusions for LandLOD, LandO, projected-shadow, point-light, SI, landlo-fog, helper, and interior-looking rows.
- Do not use selector +0xA8 == 9 or shader pair alone as sufficient proof.
